### [252] [NavOL: Navigation Policy with Online Imitation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11762)
*Xiaofei Wei,Chun Gu,Li Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为NavOL的在线模仿学习框架，用于提升机器人导航策略的稳健性，并通过与模拟器互动、在线收集专家轨迹来进行训练，展现出对离线模仿学习和强化学习的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人导航方法存在分布偏移和误差累积（离线模仿学习）、奖励函数设计复杂和学习效率低（强化学习）等问题，亟需一种兼具效率与稳健性的学习方案。

Method: NavOL基于预训练的导航扩散策略，将局部观测映射到未来航点。在训练过程中，导航策略与模拟器交互，通过调用具有全局环境信息的规划器获取最优路径作为标签，并用这些数据不断训练更新导航策略，从而避免奖励设计难题，并有效减少分布偏移。系统使用IsaacLab平台，支持并行渲染和域随机化，能高效生成大量导航数据。

Result: NavOL在50个场景、8块RTX 4090 GPU上每小时可收集2000多条长轨迹。在公开NavDP基准和新设定基准，以及真实环境实验中，NavOL表现优异，在在线模仿学习任务中持续取得性能提升。

Conclusion: NavOL系统消除了奖励工程的需求，提升了训练效率和泛化能力，并能有效减缓分布偏移，为机器人视觉导航任务提供了强有力的解决方案。

Abstract: Learning robust navigation policies remains a core challenge in robotics. Offline imitation learning suffers from distribution shift and compounding errors at rollout, while reinforcement learning requires reward engineering and learns inefficiently. In this paper, we propose NavOL, an online imitation learning paradigm that interacts with a simulator and updates itself using expert demonstrations gathered online. Built upon a pretrained navigation diffusion policy that maps local observations to future waypoints, NavOL trains in a rollout update loop: during rollout, the policy acts in the simulator and queries a global planner which has privileged access to the global environment for the optimal path segment as ground truth trajectory labels; during update, the policy is trained on the online collected observation trajectory pairs. This online imitation loop removes the need for reward design, improves learning efficiency, and mitigates distribution shift by training on the policy own explored rollouts. Built on IsaacLab with fast, high-fidelity parallel rendering and domain randomization of camera pose and start-goal pairs, our system scales across 50 scenes on 8 RTX 4090 GPUs, collecting over 2,000 new trajectories per hour, each averaging more than 400 steps. We also introduce an indoor visual navigation benchmark with predefined start and goal positions for zero-shot generalization. Extensive evaluations on simulation benchmarks, including the NavDP benchmark and our proposed benchmark, as well as carefully designed real-world experiments, demonstrate the effectiveness of NavOL, showing consistent performance gains in online imitation learning.

### [253] [See What Matters: Differentiable Grid Sample Pruning for Generalizable Vision-Language-Action Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11817)
*Yixu Feng,Zinan Zhao,Yanxiang Ma,Chenghao Xia,Chengbin Du,Yunke Wang,Chang Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的视觉-语言-动作模型视觉信息压缩方法——Differentiable Grid Sampler (GridS)，能实现极高的压缩率且无性能损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型在机器人操作任务中表现出色，但高计算成本限制了其实时部署。虽然令牌裁剪技术可以压缩计算量，但过度裁剪会丢失关键空间（如接触点）细节，导致性能严重下降，因此存在压缩率与性能的难以调和的矛盾。

Method: 作者提出GridS模块，通过可微分网格采样，针对任务自适应连续重采视觉令牌，预测最小的显著空间坐标，并通过可微插值提取关键特征。该方法保持了空间几何信息的重要性，并可极大压缩视觉令牌数量（小于10%原始令牌数）。

Result: 在LIBERO基准和真实机器人平台上实验证明，GridS在保持成功率完全不降的情况下，将视觉计算量（FLOPs）削减了76%，达到了目前最低且可行的视觉令牌数量。

Conclusion: GridS打破了VLA压缩率与性能之间的矛盾，为高效实时机器人视觉处理提供了新方法，显著减少计算成本且无性能损失。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown remarkable promise in robotics manipulation, yet their high computational cost hinders real-time deployment. Existing token pruning methods suffer from a fundamental trade-off: aggressive compression using pruning inevitably discards critical geometric details like contact points, leading to severe performance degradation. This forces a compromise, limiting the achievable compression rate and thus the potential speedup. We argue that breaking this trade-off requires rethinking compression as a geometry-aware, continuous token resampling in the vision encoder. To this end, we propose the Differentiable Grid Sampler (GridS), a plug-and-play module that performs task-aware, continuous resampling of visual tokens in VLA. By adaptively predicting a minimal set of salient coordinates and extracting features via differentiable interpolation, GridS preserves essential spatial information while achieving drastic compression (with fewer than 10% original visual tokens). Experiments on both LIBERO benchmark and a real robotic platform demonstrate that validating the lowest feasible visual token count reported to date, GridS achieves a 76% reduction in FLOPs with no degradation in the success rate. The code is available at https://github.com/Fediory/Grid-Sampler.

### [254] [Mapping Embodied Affective Touch Strategies on a Humanoid Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11825)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 招募32名参与者，与装有全身触觉传感器的iCub机器人交互。设置自由触摸、仅限手臂和仅限躯干三种条件，参与者在不同条件下表达8种情感，通过分析触摸位置、动态、压力特征以及问卷调查进行综合分析。

Result: 身体区域和空间约束共同影响触摸位置和动态。自由触摸时，参与者偏好上半身可接近区域，冷门区域的情感表达更具选择性。手臂区域更体现触摸动态的情感差异，躯干区域则呈现压力特征变化。不同条件下的触摸策略难以直接迁移。约30%参与者经历了与机器人的社会关系感知变化。

Existing HRI studies typically focus on one or two isolated body parts, limiting understanding of how affective touch generalises across the full humanoid body. We present a study with 32 participants interacting with the iCub robot, which is equipped with full-body distributed tactile sensors. Participants expressed eight emotions under three conditions: free touch, arm-only touch, and torso-only touch. Results show that body region and spatial constraints jointly shaped both touch location and dynamics. In free touch, participants preferred socially accessible upper-body regions, while less frequently touched areas showed stronger emotion-specific selectivity. Emotion-related variation was more evident in motion features for arm-only touch and pressure features for torso-only touch. Touch strategies also did not transfer directly between free and constrained conditions, even within the same coarse body region. Participants reported increased closeness to the robot after interaction, with around 30 percent reporting a change in perceived social relationship. Together, these findings show that affective touch expression is strongly body-region dependent and shaped by embodiment constraints.

To improve action learning efficiency, we introduce Action Manifold Learning (AML), which directly predicts actions on the valid action manifold, bypassing inefficient regression of unstructured targets like noise or velocity. Experiments on LIBERO, RoboTwin 2.0, and real-robot tasks show our method achieves superior success rate and robustness over SOTA baselines. In this paper, we propose EvoNav, an evolutionary framework that automates the design of robot navigation reward functions via large language models (LLMs). To overcome prohibitively costly policy training, EvoNav evaluates each candidate proposal from the LLM via a progressive three-stage warm-up-boost procedure. ### [257] [From Reaction to Anticipation: Proactive Failure Recovery through Agentic Task Graph for Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11951)
*Sheng Xu,Ruixing Jin,Huayi Zhou,Bo Yue,Guanren Qiao,Yunxin Tai,Yueci Deng,Kui Jia,Guiliang Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AgentChord是一种通过提前规划恢复策略，提升机器人操作执行可靠性与效率的新型系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人操作在面对动态与非结构化环境时，常因应对失败的流程（检测-推理-恢复）反应滞后、鲁棒性不足。受人类能够预见和主动应对潜在失败能力启发，作者希望提升操作系统的前瞻性和自主恢复能力。

Method: 提出AgentChord系统，将操作任务建模为有向图，并由三个专门Agent协作：composer负责生成基础任务图，arranger加上前瞻性恢复分支，conductor实时监控并在失败时立即切换到预设的恢复动作，无需临时规划。

Result: 大量双手操作实验表明，AgentChord显著提升了任务的成功率和执行效率。

Conclusion: AgentChord能够提高机器人在实际环境下的鲁棒性和自主性，对现实自动化系统有重要推动作用。

Abstract: Although robotic manipulation has made significant progress, reliable execution remains challenging because task failures are inevitable in dynamic and unstructured environments. To handle such failures, existing frameworks typically follow a stepwise detect-reason-recover pipeline, which often incurs high latency and limited robustness due to delayed reasoning and reactive planning. Inspired by the human capability to anticipate and proactively plan for potential failures, we introduce AgentChord, an agentic system that models a manipulation task as a directed task graph. Before execution, this graph is enriched with anticipatory recovery branches that specify context-aware corrective behaviors, enabling immediate and targeted responses when failures occur. Specifically, AgentChord operates through a choreography of specialized agents: a composer that structures the nominal task graph, an arranger that augments the graph with anticipatory recovery branches, and a conductor that compiles and coordinates executable transitions using low-latency monitors to detect deviations and trigger pre-compiled recoveries without re-planning. Empirical studies on diverse long-horizon bimanual manipulation tasks demonstrate that AgentChord substantially improves success rates and execution efficiency, advancing the reliability and autonomy of real-world robotic systems. The project page is available at: https://shengxu.net/AgentChord/.

</details>


### [258] [Cooperative Robotics Reinforced by Collective Perception for Traffic Moderation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11972)
*Mohammad Khoshkdahan,John Pravin Arockiasamy,Andy Flores Comeca,Alexey Vinel*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出在非视距（NLOS）交叉口利用协作人形机器人与集体感知系统增强交通安全，可主动阻止未联网车辆的不安全并道，实现早期预警与物理干预，降低碰撞风险，并在实地实验中证实有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在NLOS路口，因驾驶员视野受限，交通碰撞风险高。虽然V2X技术能提升安全，但普及率低且警报可能被忽视。集体感知虽能扩展联网车辆感知，但无法影响未联网车辆。因此，亟需一种能覆盖所有车辆、并可主动介入的安全措施。

Method: 提出引入协作人形机器人作为交通调解者，结合路侧双摄像头与V2X信息，通过感知融合实时检测并预测潜在碰撞风险。当探测到危险时，机器人模拟人类手势发出“STOP”信号并物理阻挡车辆。系统在鹿特丹实际交通场地进行了部署与测试。

Result: 实验结果表明，机器人结合视觉与V2X感知，能提前识别来车，准确预测碰撞风险，并有效阻止危险并道，验证了系统在现实NLOS场景下的实用性和可靠性。

Conclusion: 该混合系统补足了传统V2X和集体感知的局限，通过机器人实现主动物理干预，为提升NLOS路口交通安全提供了创新且有效的解决思路。

Abstract: Collisions at non-line-of-sight (NLOS) intersections remain a major safety concern because drivers have limited visibility of approaching traffic. V2X based warnings can reduce these risks, yet many vehicles are not equipped with V2X and drivers may ignore in vehicle alerts. Collective perception (CP) can compensate for low V2X penetration by extending the awareness of connected vehicles, but it cannot influence unconnected vehicles. To fill this gap, our work introduces a complementary concept that adds a cooperative humanoid robot as an active traffic moderator capable of physically stopping a vehicle that attempts to merge into an unseen traffic stream. The system operates on two parallel perception pathways. A dual camera infrastructure unit detects the position, speed and motion of approaching vehicles and transmits this information to the robot as a collective perception message (CPM). The robot also receives cooperative awareness messages (CAM) from connected vehicles through its onboard V2X unit and can act as a relay for decentralized environmental notification messages (DENM) when safety events originate elsewhere along the road. A fusion module combines these streams to maintain a robust real time view of the main road. A Zone of Danger (ZoD) is defined and used to predict whether an approaching vehicle creates a collision risk for a merging road user. When such a risk is detected, the robot issues a human-like STOP gesture and blocks the merging path until the hazard disappears. The full system was deployed at the Future Mobility Park (FMP) in Rotterdam. Experiments show that the combined vision and V2X perception allows the robot to detect approaching vehicles early, predict hazards reliably and prevent unsafe merges in real world NLOS conditions.

### [259] [Closing the Motion Execution Gap: From Semantic Motion Task Constraints to Kinematic Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12053)
*Simon Stelter,Vanessa Hassouna,Malte Huerkamp,Michael Beetz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了Motion Statecharts，一种符号化可执行的运动表示方法，实现从任务描述到机器人动作的无缝衔接，并在多个平台验证了其实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人高层语义任务与具体动作执行之间存在断层（Motion Execution Gap），难以直接将任务要求转化为机器人可用的动作指令。

Method: 提出Motion Statecharts表示，允许运动约束、监控和嵌套状态图的并行与顺序组合。核心是基于可微分统一运动学世界模型，实现跨平台、环境的广义动作规范。通过lMPC方法实现运动控制，并用jerk边界保证任务切换的平滑性。

Result: 该方法已在八种不同机器人平台和多样环境下验证，能够跨平台迁移动作规范。

Conclusion: Motion Statecharts有效连接高层任务与机器人运动控制，提升机器人的灵活性和通用性，Giskard框架已开源。

Abstract: This paper addresses the Motion Execution Gap, the disconnect between high-level symbolic task descriptions using semantic constraints and executable robot motions. Motion Statecharts are introduced as an executable symbolic representation for complex motions. They allow the arbitrary arrangement of motion constraints, monitors or nested statecharts in parallel and sequence. World-centric motion specification and generalization across embodiments are enabled through the use of a unified differentiable kinematic world model of both, robots and environments. Motion execution is realized through a lMPC-based implementation of the task-function approach, in which smooth transitions during task switches are ensured using jerk bounds. Cross-platform transferability was demonstrated by deploying the method on eight robot platforms, operating in diverse environments. The proposed framework is called Giskard and is available open source: https://github.com/cram2/cognitive_robot_abstract_machine.

</details>


### [260] [Control of Fully Actuated Aerial Vehicles: A Comparison of Model-based and Sensor-based Dynamic Inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12071)
*Ali Sidar Yilmaz,Buday Turan,Lukas Pries,Markus Ryll*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文比较了两种六旋翼全驱无人机的控制器：基于模型的非线性动态反演（NDI）与基于传感器的增量动态反演（INDI）。实验结果显示，在模型失配、风干扰、传感器退化等情况下，INDI性能更优，但降采样时NDI姿态跟踪更好。该工作首次验证了全姿态跟踪下INDI控制器的实验效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全驱多旋翼无人机因实现位置与姿态的独立控制，提升了飞行机动性，但对控制器的鲁棒性和实时性提出更高要求。本文旨在探究模型驱动与传感器驱动的反演控制策略，在实际平台中谁更适合鲁棒高效地控制全驱无人机。

Method: 在同一全驱六旋翼平台上，设计并实现了模型驱动的几何NDI和传感器驱动的INDI控制器，两者外环结构一致，内环分别采用动态反演。通过姿态跟踪、扰动抑制、风干扰、降采样、传感器退化等5项实验，系统比较其性能。

Result: INDI在模型参数误差、外部扰动、传感器退化及控制频率降低时，均表现出更高的稳态精度和鲁棒性。但在控制频率降低场景，几何NDI有更好的姿态跟踪。

Conclusion: 两种控制策略各有优劣。INDI适合应对实际环境中的不确定性，对鲁棒性和部署要求高的全驱无人机更有优势。而NDI在系统频率资源受限时仍能保证高质量姿态跟踪，强调两者在工程落地时的权衡。

Abstract: Fully actuated multirotor platforms decouple translational force generation from vehicle attitude, enabling independent control of position and orientation and shifting performance limitations from attitude authority to actuator dynamics and control effectiveness. This paper compares a model-based nonlinear dynamic inversion controller (geometric NDI) with a sensor-based incremental dynamic inversion controller (INDI) on a fixed-tilt fully actuated hexarotor. Both controllers share an identical outer-loop structure and are both executed at 500 Hz; therefore, performance differences can be attributed primarily to the inversion strategy. Controller performance is evaluated in five experiments covering attitude step tracking under nominal conditions and under a 50% mismatch in the rotor force coefficient, hover disturbance rejection under an external lateral load, waypoint tracking in the presence of wind gust disturbances, reduced control frequency, and injected sensor degradation. The results show that INDI offers clear advantages under parameter mismatch, gust disturbances, and sensor degradation, and maintains lower position errors across the controller-frequency sweep. However, its advantages are not universal: geometric NDI yields better attitude tracking at reduced control frequencies. To the authors' best knowledge, this work presents the first experimental validation of a full pose tracking INDI controller with decoupled translational and rotational dynamics. These findings highlight the trade-off between measurement-based and model-based inversion for robust control and rapid deployment of fully actuated UAVs.

### [261] [Learning What Matters: Adaptive Information-Theoretic Objectives for Robot Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12084)
*Youwei Yu,Jionghao Wang,Zhengming Yu,Wenping Wang,Lantao Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的类最优实验设计方法（QOED），通过选择可观测的参数方向和抑制无关参数影响，提高机器人探索效率，在仿真与真实任务中显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人探索任务中，当前信息论目标难以有效反映参数可学习性，尤其是在高维系统下，许多参数难以观测或辨认，且无关参数会扭曲探索目标，从而影响机器人学习效率。

Method: 提出QOED方法，利用Fisher信息矩阵进行特征空间分析，自动选取可辨认参数方向，并调整探索目标，强化在这些方向上的信息获取，同时抑制无关参数的负面效应，在一定假设下实现对理想信息目标的常数因子近似。

Result: 在多项仿真和真实机器人导航及操作任务中，QOED分别通过可辨认方向选择和无关参数抑制带来35.23%和21.98%的性能提升，在集成到基于模型的策略优化后，进一步优于传统强化学习基线。

Conclusion: QOED通过聚焦于可辨认参数方向，有效提升了机器人探索和策略优化的效果，为高维机器人系统中的信息论目标设计提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Designing learnable information-theoretic objectives for robot exploration remains challenging. Such objectives aim to guide exploration toward data that reduces uncertainty in model parameters, yet it is often unclear what information the collected data can actually reveal. Although reinforcement learning (RL) can optimize a given objective, constructing objectives that reflect parametric learnability is difficult in high-dimensional robotic systems. Many parameter directions are weakly observable or unidentifiable, and even when identifiable directions are selected, omitted directions can still influence exploration and distort information measures. To address this challenge, we propose Quasi-Optimal Experimental Design (Q{\footnotesize OED}), an adaptive information objective grounded in optimal experimental design. Q{\footnotesize OED} (i) performs eigenspace analysis of the Fisher information matrix to identify an observable subspace and select identifiable parameter directions, and (ii) modifies the exploration objective to emphasize these directions while suppressing nuisance effects from non-critical parameters. Under bounded nuisance influence and limited coupling between critical and nuisance directions, Q{\footnotesize OED} provides a constant-factor approximation to the ideal information objective that explores all parameters. We evaluate Q{\footnotesize OED} on simulated and real-world navigation and manipulation tasks, where identifiable-direction selection and nuisance suppression yield performance improvements of \SI{35.23}{\percent} and \SI{21.98}{\percent}, respectively. When integrated as an exploration objective in model-based policy optimization, Q{\footnotesize OED} further improves policy performance over established RL baselines.

### [262] [World Action Models: The Next Frontier in Embodied AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12090)
*Siyin Wang,Junhao Shi,Zhaoyang Fu,Xinzhe He,Feihong Liu,Chenchen Yang,Yikang Zhou,Zhaoye Fei,Jingjing Gong,Jinlan Fu,Mike Zheng Shou,Xuanjing Huang,Xipeng Qiu,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文对“世界动作模型（WAMs）”进行了首次系统性的综述，明确其定义、架构分类、数据生态、评测方式以及面临的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型虽能实现良好的语义泛化，但仅实现了对观测到动作的反应式映射，未对环境动力变化进行显式建模。为提升智能体对物理世界演化的建模，研究者正将世界模型（环境动力学预测模型）引入动作生成过程，形成WAMs这一新兴范式，但相关研究尚缺统一的概念框架和系统梳理。

Method: 作者首先明确WAMs的正式定义，厘清其与相关概念的区别。随后，依据现有文献提出了包含层级式（Cascaded）和联合式（Joint）两大类WAMs的结构化分类体系，并进一步细分生成方式、条件设定、动作解码等特征。同时，系统分析了驱动WAMs发展的数据源，包括机器人遥操作、人类示范、仿真及大规模主观视频等，归纳整理了以视觉一致性、物理常识与动作合理性为核心的评测标准。

Result: 文中梳理和归纳出WAMs主要的架构范式及其权衡，提出全面检测与评价体系，系统揭示了WAMs发展的动力、现状与趋势。

Conclusion: 本综述为世界动作模型（WAMs）领域提供了系统化的理论基础和分类框架，细化了架构选择与评估，明确开放问题，为推动该领域创新与实际应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have achieved strong semantic generalization for embodied policy learning, yet they learn reactive observation-to-action mappings without explicitly modeling how the physical world evolves under intervention. A growing body of work addresses this limitation by integrating world models, predictive models of environment dynamics, into the action generation pipeline. We term this emerging paradigm World Action Models (WAMs): embodied foundation models that unify predictive state modeling with action generation, targeting a joint distribution over future states and actions rather than actions alone. However, the literature remains fragmented across architectures, learning objectives, and application scenarios, lacking a unified conceptual framework. We formally define WAMs and disambiguate them from related concepts, and trace the foundations and early integration of VLA and world model research that gave rise to this paradigm. We organize existing methods into a structured taxonomy of Cascaded and Joint WAMs, with further subdivision by generation modality, conditioning mechanism, and action decoding strategy. We systematically analyze the data ecosystem fueling WAMs development, spanning robot teleoperation, portable human demonstrations, simulation, and internet-scale egocentric video, and synthesize emerging evaluation protocols organized around visual fidelity, physical commonsense, and action plausibility. Overall, this survey provides the first systematic account of the WAMs landscape, clarifies key architectural paradigms and their trade-offs, and identifies open challenges and future opportunities for this rapidly evolving field.

</details>


### [263] [Premover: Fast Vision-Language-Action Control by Acting Before Instructions Are Complete](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12160)
*Joonha Park,Jiseung Jeong,Taesik Gong*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了Premover模块，通过在用户输入请求期间预处理视觉和语言信息，提高机器人响应速度，同时保持任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略在用户请求输入过程期间未充分利用等待时间，导致实际部署时整体交互效率低下。

Method: Premover在不改变VLA主干网络参数的前提下，新增两个小型映射头，分别针对图像和语言，将中间层特征映射到共享空间，生成关注图，并以目标分割蒙版为监督。通过一个可联合训练的准备阈值，动态决定机器人何时开始动作。

Result: 在LIBERO基准套件上，Premover将平均交互总用时从34.0秒缩短到29.4秒，减少13.6%，且成功率与完整请求输入下的基线几乎一致（95.1% vs. 95.0%），而天真的预处理方法成功率仅为66.4%。

Conclusion: Premover能够有效利用用户输入期间的空闲时间进行有用的预计算，显著提升VLA策略实际部署中的交互效率，且不损失任务成功率。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies are typically evaluated as if the user had finished typing or speaking before the robot begins acting. In real deployment, however, users take several seconds to enter a request, leaving the policy idle for a substantial fraction of the interaction. We introduce Premover, a lightweight module that converts this idle window into useful precomputation. Premover keeps the VLA backbone frozen and attaches two small projection heads, one for image patches, one for language tokens, that map an intermediate layer of the backbone into a shared space. The resulting focus map is supervised by simulator-rendered target-object segmentation masks and applied as a per-patch reweighting of the next step's image tokens. A single scalar readiness threshold, trained jointly from streaming prefixes, decides when the policy should begin acting. On the LIBERO benchmark suite, Premover reduces mean wall-clock time from 34.0 to 29.4 seconds, a 13.6% reduction, while matching the full-prompt baseline's success rate (95.1% vs. 95.0%); naive premoving, by contrast, collapses to 66.4%.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在24个仿真和3个真实任务中的大量实验表明，该框架在性能上显著优于既有基础策略和先前采用显式姿态指导的方法。

Existing methods typically treat spatial perception and action execution as decoupled or strictly unidirectional processes, fundamentally restricting a robot's ability to master complex manipulation tasks. To address this, we propose X-Imitator, a versatile dual-path framework that models spatial perception and action execution as a tightly coupled bidirectional loop. By reciprocally conditioning current pose predictions on past actions and vice versa, this framework enables continuous mutual refinement between spatial reasoning and action generation. This joint modeling exactly mimics human internal forward models. Designed as a modular architecture, the system can be seamlessly integrated into various visuomotor policies. Extensive experiments across 24 simulated and 3 real-world tasks demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms both vanilla policies and prior methods utilizing explicit pose guidance. The code will be open sourced.

### [265] [From Imagined Futures to Executable Actions: Mixture of Latent Actions for Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12167)
*Yajie Li,Bozhou Zhang,Chun Gu,Zipei Ma,Jiahui Zhang,Jiankang Deng,Xiatian Zhu,Li Zhang*

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的方法MoLA，将视频生成模型的想象能力转化为可执行动作表示，用于提升机器人操作任务的执行效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成与动作决策耦合不良，生成的视频强调视觉真实感而忽略了与动作相关的物理转换，导致机器人控制不稳定、效果有限。

Method: 引入MoLA接口，通过一组预训练的逆动力学模型从视频转换中推断隐式的混合动作。这些模型利用语义、深度和流等多种模态信息，融合后得到结构化的动作表示，从而使视频预测结果更适合动作执行。

Result: 在仿真（LIBERO, CALVIN, LIBERO-Plus等）和真实机器人操作任务上，MoLA方法相比直接基于视频预测的方法，表现出更高的任务完成率、更好的时序一致性和更强的泛化能力。

Abstract: Video generation models offer a promising imagination mechanism for robot manipulation by predicting long-horizon future observations, but effectively exploiting these imagined futures for action execution remains challenging. Existing approaches either condition policies on predicted frames or directly decode generated videos into actions, both suffering from a mismatch between visual realism and control relevance. As a result, predicted observations emphasize perceptual fidelity rather than action-centric causes of state transitions, leading to indirect and unstable control. To address this gap, we propose MoLA (Mixture of Latent Actions), a control-oriented interface that transforms imagined future videos into executable representations. Instead of passing predicted frames directly to the policy, MoLA leverages a mixture of pretrained inverse dynamics models to infer a mixture of latent actions implied by generated visual transitions. These modality-aware inverse dynamics models capture complementary semantic, depth, and flow cues, providing a structured and physically grounded action representation that bridges video imagination and policy execution. We evaluate our approach on simulated benchmarks (LIBERO, CALVIN, and LIBERO-Plus) and real-world robot manipulation tasks, achieving consistent gains in task success, temporal consistency, and generalization.

### [266] [DexTwist: Dexterous Hand Retargeting for Twist Motion via Mixed Reality-based Teleoperation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12182)
*Dongmyoung Lee,Chengxi Li,Dongheui Lee*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了DexTwist，一种针对MR（混合现实）远程灵巧操作的功能性扭转重定向框架，能显著改善机器人灵巧手在接触丰富旋转操作（如拧瓶盖、拧钥匙等）中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的灵巧手远程操作通过最小化运动学差异（如关节角度或指尖位置误差）进行动作重定向，但由于人与机器手在结构上的差异，容易导致指尖打滑、旋转轴漂移、抓握不稳定等问题，难以实现复杂的旋转操作。

Method: 作者提出DexTwist框架，实时检测用户三指捏持动作，估算意图旋转轴和旋转量，并在运动过程中结合三指架构进行残差关节空间优化，通过虚拟物体目标函数（包括旋转角、旋转轴一致性、指尖闭合和三指稳定性）对操作进行调节。

Result: 通过仿真和真实实验，DexTwist实现了比传统基于矢量的重定向方法更稳定的旋转轴跟踪和旋转角控制。

Conclusion: DexTwist能有效地桥接MR远程操控中由于硬件差异带来的体现鸿沟，提升机器人完成复杂旋转抓取任务的能力。

Abstract: Dexterous teleoperation via Mixed Reality (MR)-based interfaces offers a scalable paradigm for transferring human manipulation skills to dexterous robot hands. However, conventional retargeting approaches that minimize kinematic dissimilarity (e.g., joint angle or fingertip position error) often fail in contact-rich rotational manipulation, such as cap opening, key turning, and bolt screwing. This failure stems from the embodiment gap: mismatched link lengths, joint axes/limits, and fingertip geometry can cause direct pose imitation to induce tangential fingertip sliding rather than stable object rotation, resulting in screw axis drift, contact slip, and grasp instability. To address this, we propose DexTwist, a functional twist-retargeting framework for MR-based dexterous teleoperation. DexTwist detects a tripod pinch, estimates the operator's intended screw axis and twist magnitude, and applies a real-time residual joint-space refinement that tracks turning progress while regularizing the robot tripod geometry. The refinement minimizes a virtual-object objective defined by turning angle, screw axis consistency, fingertip closure, and tripod stability. Simulation and real-world experiments show that DexTwist improves turning angle tracking and screw axis stability compared with a vector-based retargeting baseline.

</details>


### [267] [Morphologically Equivariant Flow Matching for Bimanual Mobile Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12228)
*Max Siebenborn,Daniel Ordoñez Apraez,Sophie Lueth,Giulio Turrisi,Massimiliano Pontil,Claudio Semini,Georgia Chalvatzaki*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出利用机器人本体对称性促进双臂移动操作学习的新方法，并在多种任务和实际机器人上验证其显著提升泛化能力和数据效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常规模仿学习忽视了双臂机器人的本体左右对称性，而这种对称意味着对一侧的任务解法可以直接推广到镜像配置。本文指出这种对称作为归纳偏置可以提升学习效率与泛化性。

Method: 作者形式化提出本体对称性作为先验约束，通过引入$C_2$-等变流匹配策略（flow matching policy）实现反射对称性。具体方法包括损失函数正则化与等变速度网络两种实现途径。

Result: 在平面和6-DoF的双臂移动操作任务中，嵌入对称性归纳偏置的策略不仅提升了样本效率，还能零样本泛化到训练集中未见过的镜像任务配置。还在TIAGo++真实机器人上验证了该方法的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 形态对称性是一种普适可扩展的有用归纳偏置，可有效提升双臂机器人仿生泛化与本领迁移性能，为无先验配置下的策略学习提供强有力的理论与实践基础。

Abstract: Mobile manipulation requires coordinated control of high-dimensional, bimanual robots. Imitation learning methods have been broadly used to solve these robotic tasks, yet typically ignore the bilateral morphological symmetry inherent in such systems. We argue that morphological symmetry is an underexplored but crucial inductive bias for learning in bimanual mobile manipulation: knowing how to solve a task in one configuration directly determines how to solve its mirrored counterpart. In this paper, we formalize this symmetry prior and show that it constrains optimal bimanual policies to be ambidextrous and equivariant under reflections across the robot's sagittal plane. We introduce a $\mathbb{C}_2$-equivariant flow matching policy that enforces reflective symmetry either via a regularized training loss or an equivariant velocity network. Across planar and 6-DoF mobile manipulation tasks, symmetry-informed policies consistently improve sample efficiency and achieve zero-shot generalization to mirrored configurations absent from the training distribution. We further validate this zero-shot generalization capability on a real-world manipulation task with a TIAGo++ robot. Together, our findings establish morphological symmetry as an effective, generalizable, and scalable inductive bias for ambidextrous generative policy learning.

</details>


### [268] [TMRL: Diffusion Timestep-Modulated Pretraining Enables Exploration for Efficient Policy Finetuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12236)
*Matthew M. Hong,Jesse Zhang,Anusha Nagabandi,Abhishek Gupta*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一个结合行为克隆预训练和强化学习微调的方法，通过对输入加噪声提升探索能力，并引入时间步调制机制动态调整探索程度，显著提升了机器人策略微调的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于行为克隆的预训练方法会导致策略的动作分布窄，后续用强化学习微调时探索不充分，效率低，需要更好融合预训练和微调以提升效果。

Method: 提出Context-Smoothed Pre-training (CSP)，在行为克隆预训练时对输入加向前扩散噪声，拓宽动作覆盖。然后用Timestep-Modulated RL (TMRL)进行微调，通过动态调节扩散时间步控制探索范围。该方法适用于多种输入类型，如状态、点云或图像。

Result: 实验表明，该方法提升了强化学习微调的采样效率，并且在复杂的真实世界操作任务中，能在一小时内完成高效微调。

Conclusion: 提出的TMRL方法为机器人策略微调带来显著探索性与效率提升，对实际复杂场景有良好应用效果和通用性。

Abstract: Fine-tuning pre-trained robot policies with reinforcement learning (RL) often inherits the bottlenecks introduced by pre-training with behavioral cloning (BC), which produces narrow action distributions that lack the coverage necessary for downstream exploration. We present a unified framework that enables the exploration necessary to enable efficient robot policy finetuning by bridging BC pre-training and RL fine-tuning. Our pre-training method, Context-Smoothed Pre-training (CSP), injects forward-diffusion noise into policy inputs, creating a continuum between precise imitation and broad action coverage. We then fine-tune pre-trained policies via Timestep-Modulated Reinforcement Learning (TMRL), which trains the agent to dynamically adjust this conditioning during fine-tuning by modulating the diffusion timestep, granting explicit control over exploration. Integrating seamlessly with arbitrary policy inputs, e.g., states, 3D point clouds, or image-based VLA policies, we show that TMRL improves RL fine-tuning sample efficiency. Notably, TMRL enables successful real-world fine-tuning on complex manipulation tasks in under one hour. Videos and code available at https://weirdlabuw.github.io/tmrl/.

</details>


### [269] [SI-Diff: A Framework for Learning Search and High-Precision Insertion with a Force-Domain Diffusion Policy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12247)
*Yibo Liu,Stanko Oparnica,Simon Shewchun-Jakaitis,Guoyi Fu,Jie Wang,Jun Yang,Anand Jagannathan,Tony Hong-Yau Lo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了SI-Diff框架，通过力域扩散策略统一学习拆分解决的搜索与高精度插入两种装配任务，有效提升机器人peg-in-hole等装配容错能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前机器人装配任务中，因零件相对位姿的不确定性（如偏差和间隙过小），导致装配过程复杂。现有方法往往将搜索与高精度插入分开建模，难以统一支持智能装配系统中的全流程需求。

Method: 提出“SI-Diff”框架，利用力域扩散策略，通过引入新的条件机制，使一个策略能同时学习并区分搜索与插入动作模式。同时设计了新的search teacher policy，以生成多样化演示轨迹，无需切换模型即可适应不同装配阶段。训练阶段，模型基于这些高效成功演示数据，将触觉与末端速度映射为有效动作。

Result: 实验显示，SI-Diff相较主流基线TacDiffusion，将x-y方向的错位容忍度从2毫米提升到5毫米，并且具备良好的零样本泛化能力，能适应未见过的零件形状。

Conclusion: SI-Diff有效突破了装配过程中模型切换的问题，实现了搜索与高精度插入的统一，提升了容错性和泛化能力，为智能机器人装配提供了更高效、鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Contact-rich assembly is fundamental in robotics but poses significant challenges due to uncertainties in relative poses, such as misalignments and small clearances in peg-in-hole tasks. Existing approaches typically address search and high-precision insertion separately, because these tasks involve distinct action patterns. However, supporting both tasks within a single model, without switching models or weights, is desirable for intelligent assembly systems. In this work, we propose SI-Diff, a framework that learns both search and high-precision insertion through a force-domain diffusion policy. To this end, we introduce a new mode-conditioning mechanism that enables the policy to capture distinct action behaviors under a single framework. Moreover, we develop a new search teacher policy that can generate diverse trajectories. By training on successful and efficient demonstrations provided by the teacher policy, the model learns the mapping from tactile and end-effector velocity observations to effective action behaviors. We conduct thorough experiments to show that SI-Diff extends the tolerance to x-y misalignments from 2 mm to 5 mm compared to the state-of-the-art baseline, TacDiffusion, while also demonstrating strong zero-shot transferability to unseen shapes.

</details>


### [270] [Real-Time Whole-Body Teleoperation of a Humanoid Robot Using IMU-Based Motion Capture with Sim2Sim and Sim2Real Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12347)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前人形机器人全身遥操作在解决人体与机器人运动学不匹配、惯性传感噪声积累、控制延迟以及仿真到实际的迁移等方面存在诸多挑战，缺乏实时、稳定的工程解决方案。

Method: 作者设计了基于Virdyn IMU全身动捕服的数据采集系统，并开发了自定义的运动处理、运动学重定向及控制流程，实现了无需离线缓冲或基于学习的模块即可连续、低延迟地将人体动作映射至机器人动作。系统先在MuJoCo仿真环境中验证，再直接迁移到物理机器人上。

Result: 实验显示，系统能稳定且同步地重现包括行走、站立、坐下、转身、鞠躬、全身协调体态等多种人类动作；并实现了从仿真到实际平台无修改迁移。

Conclusion: 该工作提出并验证了一种实用、可扩展的人形机器人全身遥操作框架，可直接利用商用人体动捕硬件实现复杂动作映射，具有良好的工程意义和应用前景。

Abstract: Stable, low-latency whole-body teleoperation of humanoid robots is an open research challenge, complicated by kinematic mismatches between human and robot morphologies, accumulated inertial sensor noise, non-trivial control latency, and persistent sim-to-real transfer gaps. This paper presents a complete real-time whole-body teleoperation system that maps human motion, recorded with a Virdyn IMU-based full-body motion capture suit, directly onto a Unitree G1 humanoid robot. We introduce a custom motion-processing, kinematic retargeting, and control pipeline engineered for continuous, low-latency operation without any offline buffering or learning-based components. The system is first validated in simulation using the MuJoCo physics model of the Unitree G1 (sim2sim), and then deployed without modification on the physical platform (sim2real). Experimental results demonstrate stable, synchronized reproduction of a broad motion repertoire, including walking, standing, sitting, turning, bowing, and coordinated expressive full-body gestures. This work establishes a practical, scalable framework for whole-body humanoid teleoperation using commodity wearable motion capture hardware.

### [271] [GuidedVLA: Specifying Task-Relevant Factors via Plug-and-Play Action Attention Specialization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12369)
*Xiaosong Jia,Bowen Yang,Zuhao Ge,Xian Nie,Yuchen Zhou,Cunxin Fan,Yufeng Li,Yilin Chai,Chao Jing,Zijian Liang,Qingwen Bu,Haidong Cao,Chao Wu,Qifeng Li,Zhenjie Yang,Chenhe Zhang,Hongyang Li,Zuxuan Wu,Junchi Yan,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了GuidedVLA，一种通过显式引导提升机器人视觉-语言-动作模型泛化能力的新框架。该方法通过对动作解码器中的注意力头进行人工辅助信号监督，使其聚焦于关键任务因素，并在多个实验中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型依赖端到端监督，但缺乏对动作生成过程的显式指导，导致模型易陷入偶然关联（如视觉捷径或环境噪声），限制了其泛化能力。为了解决这一瓶颈，作者提出需明确引导模型关注与任务相关的因素。

Method: GuidedVLA将动作解码器视为由多个功能性组件（即注意力头）组成的结构，并为每个头手动定义辅助监督信号。本初步工作选取三类专门的注意力头——对象定位、空间几何和时间技能逻辑，并在模拟环境及真实机器人实验中评估该方法。

Result: GuidedVLA在域内和跨域场景的任务成功率上均显著优于现有强VLA基线。此外，实验表明，专门关注的任务相关因素质量与实际任务表现正相关，验证了解耦特征的有效性。

Conclusion: 对动作解码过程的显式指导是提升VLA模型鲁棒性和泛化能力的有效方向。GuidedVLA显示了通过组件化和辅助信号监督可以构建更健壮和通用的机器人学习模型。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models aim for general robot learning by aligning action as a modality within powerful Vision-Language Models (VLMs). Existing VLAs rely on end-to-end supervision to implicitly enable the action decoding process to learn task-relevant features. However, without explicit guidance, these models often overfit to spurious correlations, such as visual shortcuts or environmental noise, limiting their generalization. In this paper, we introduce GuidedVLA, a framework designed to manually guide the action generation to focus on task-relevant factors. Our core insight is to treat the action decoder not as a monolithic learner, but as an assembly of functional components. Individual attention heads are supervised by manually defined auxiliary signals to capture distinct factors. As an initial study, we instantiate this paradigm with three specialized heads: object grounding, spatial geometry, and temporal skill logic. Across simulation and real-robot experiments, GuidedVLA improves success rates in both in-domain and out-of-domain settings compared to strong VLA baselines. Finally, we show that the quality of these specialized factors correlates positively with task performance and that our mechanism yields decoupled, high-quality features. Our results suggest that explicitly guiding action-decoder learning is a promising direction for building more robust and general VLA models.

</details>


### [272] [SafeManip: A Property-Driven Benchmark for Temporal Safety Evaluation in Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12386)
*Chengyue Huang,Khang Vo Huynh,Sebastian Elbaum,Zsolt Kira,Lu Feng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出SafeManip基准，用于显式评估机器人操作中的时序安全性，弥补以往只关注任务完成度的不足。通过LTLf模板及符号跟踪，系统地检测八类安全属性在六种策略与50项任务中的表现，发现即使先进模型仍常违背安全性，任务成功并不等于执行安全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人操作主要只考量任务是否完成，忽视了执行过程中潜在的时序性安全风险（如二次污染、过早释放等）。缺乏通用并可复用的安全标准去评估操作的“安全完成”，尤其在复杂或长时任务中暴露突出。

Method: SafeManip通过有限轨迹线性时序逻辑（LTLf）定义多种可复用安全性模板，把实际机器人操作过程转换为符号谓词轨迹，并用LTLf监控程序自动检测八类安全事件。模板可针对不同任务和环境快速实例化。作者对六种主流视觉-语言-动作策略及多个任务开展了系统验证。

Result: 实验结果表明，即便是任务成功率较高的先进策略，其操作过程中的安全性表现依然不理想。任务完成≠安全执行，许多成功执行中实际存在安全违规，而且任务越复杂/越长，安全违规越普遍。SafeManip能有效发现并量化这些易被忽视的问题。

Conclusion: SafeManip为机器人操作研究和落地提供了可推广的安全评估工具，使研究者/开发者能超越简单的任务完成率，更准确地衡量真实世界中的安全表现，促进更可靠的机器人技术发展。

Abstract: Robotic manipulation is typically evaluated by task success, but successful completion does not guarantee safe execution. Many safety failures are temporal: a robot may touch a clean surface after contamination or release an object before it is fully inside an enclosure. We introduce SafeManip, a property-driven benchmark to explicitly evaluate temporal safety properties in robotic manipulation, moving beyond prior evaluations that largely focus on task completion or per-state constraint violations. SafeManip defines reusable safety templates over finite executions using Linear Temporal Logic over finite traces (LTLf). It maps observed rollouts to symbolic predicate traces and evaluates them with LTLf-based monitors. Its property suite covers eight manipulation safety categories: collision and contact safety, grasp stability, release stability, cross-contamination, action onset, mechanism recovery, object containment, and enclosure access. Templates can be instantiated with task-specific objects, fixtures, regions, or skills, allowing the same safety specifications to generalize across tasks and environments. We evaluate SafeManip on six vision-language-action policies, including $π_0$, $π_{0.5}$, GR00T, and their training variants, across 50 RoboCasa365 household tasks. Results show that even strong models often behave unsafely. Task-success gains do not reliably translate into safer execution: many successful rollouts remain unsafe, while longer-horizon or more complex tasks expose more violations. SafeManip provides a reusable evaluation layer for diagnosing temporal safety failures and measuring safe success beyond task completion.

</details>
